# API Specification — Veeam ONE REST API

> Generated by `api2md.py` from a OpenAPI 3.0.1 spec. https://github.com/JoshFinlayAU/apilearn

## 1. Overview

- **Version:** 2.3
- **Operations:** 281 across 19 resource groups
- **Reusable schemas:** see [§5](#schemas) — referenced throughout §4 via links.

## 2. Authentication

- **Bearer** — `apiKey` `Authorization` in header
- **Applied globally:** Bearer

<a id="conventions"></a>
## 3. Conventions (inferred)

- **Success response envelope:** most 2xx bodies wrap data in `{ items, totalCount }`.
- **Status codes in use:** 200 (×281), 204 (×1), 400 (×10), 403 (×279), 422 (×2)
- **Path naming:** lowercase, camelOrPascal, plural-noun
- **Query params (all, by frequency):** `Offset`, `Limit`, `Filter`, `Sort`, `Select`
- **Request content types:** `application/json`, `application/x-www-form-urlencoded`, `multipart/form-data`
- **Response content types:** `application/json`

## 4. Endpoints

### About

- **`GET /api/v2.3/about`** — Get Veeam ONE Server Information
  - operationId: `About_GetAbout`
  - responses: 200→[`ServerInformation`](#schema-ServerInformation), 403→[`ProblemDetails`](#schema-ProblemDetails)
- **`GET /api/v2.3/about/installationInfo`** — Get Veeam ONE Installation Information
  - operationId: `About_GetServiceInfo`
  - responses: 200→[`VeeamOneServiceInfo`](#schema-VeeamOneServiceInfo), 403→[`ProblemDetails`](#schema-ProblemDetails)
- **`POST /api/v2.3/about/logs`** — Collect Log Archive
  - operationId: `About_StartVeeamOneLogsTask`
  - body: { fromDate?: string(date-time) }
  - responses: 200→[`AsyncTaskStatus`](#schema-AsyncTaskStatus), 403→[`ProblemDetails`](#schema-ProblemDetails)
- **`POST /api/v2.3/about/logs/tasks/{taskId}/status`** — Get Log Archive Collection Task
  - operationId: `About_GetVeeamOneLogsTaskStatus`
  - path params: `taskId*`:`string(uuid)`
  - responses: 200→[`AsyncTaskStatus`](#schema-AsyncTaskStatus), 403→[`ProblemDetails`](#schema-ProblemDetails)

#### `AccessTokenRole`
`enum("Unknown", "Admin", "PowerUser", "ReadonlyUser", "Tenant", "DashboardViewer", "ReportViewer", "Service", "VbrApplication", "VdroApplication", "ChatBotAdvanced", "ChatBotBase")`

<a id="schema-AgentBackupJobInfo"></a>
#### `AgentBackupJobInfo`
| field | type | required | description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `agentBackupJobUid` | `string(uuid)` | no | UID assigned to a job in Veeam Backup & Replication. |
| `backupServerId` | `integer(int64)` | no | ID assigned to a Veeam Backup & Replication server. |
| `status` | `enum("Unknown", "None", "Success", "Warning", "Failed", "Running")` | no | Job status. |
| `details` | `string[]` | no | Additional information on a job. |
| `name` | `string` | no | Name of a job. |
| `description` | `string` | no | Job description. |
| `platform` | `enum("Unknown", "MicrosoftWindows", "Linux", "Mac", "IbmAix", "OracleSolaris", "IbmAixOracleSolaris", "Custom")` | no | Platform of Veeam backup agents. |
| `lastRun` | `string(date-time)` | no | Date and time of the latest job session. |
| `lastRunDurationSec` | `integer(int32)` | no | Duration of the latest job session, in seconds. |
| `avgDurationSec` | `integer(int32)` | no | Average job session duration, in seconds. |
| `lastTransferredDataBytes` | `integer(int64)` | no | Amount of data transferred during the latest job session, in bytes. |

| field | type | required | description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `items` | [`AgentBackupJobInfo[]`](#schema-AgentBackupJobInfo) | no |  |
| `totalCount` | `integer(int32)` | no |  |

| `name` | `string` | no | Name of a job. |
| `agentPolicyUid` | `string(uuid)` | no | UID assigned to a parent Veeam backup agent policy in Veeam Backup & Replication. |
| `computerName` | `string` | no | Name of a computer protected by a job. |
| `protectedAgentUid` | `string(uuid)` | no | UID assigned to a Veeam backup agent installed on a protected computer. |
| `ipAddresses` | `string[]` | no | IP addresses of a protected computer. |
| `backupServerId` | `integer(int64)` | no | ID assigned to a Veeam Backup & Replication server. |
| `status` | `enum("Unknown", "None", "Success", "Warning", "Failed", "Running")` | no | Status of a job. |
| `details` | `string[]` | no | Additional information on a job. |
| `lastRun` | `string(date-time)` | no | Date and time of the latest job session. |
| `lastRunDurationSec` | `integer(int32)` | no | Duration of the latest job session, in seconds. |
| `avgDurationSec` | `integer(int32)` | no | Average job session duration, in seconds. |
| `lastTransferredDataBytes` | `integer(int64)` | no | Amount of data transferred during the latest job session, in bytes. |

| `backupServerId` | `integer(int64)` | no | ID assigned to a Veeam Backup & Replication server. |

| `type` | `enum("Unknown", "MicrosoftWindows", "Linux", "SMB", "DellEMCDataDomain", "HPEStoreOnce", "ExaGrid", "Cloud", "QuantumDXi", "LinuxHardened", "NFS")` | no | Type of a backup repository. |
| `capacityBytes` | `integer(int64)` | no | Storage capacity of a backup repository, in bytes. |
| `freeSpaceBytes` | `integer(int64)` | no | Amount of free storage space on the repository, in bytes. |
| `runningTasks` | `integer(int32)` | no | Number of tasks that are currently running on a backup repository. |
| `maxConcurrentTasks` | `integer(int32)` | no | Maximum number of concurrent tasks allowed for a backup proxy. |
| `upgradeRequired` | `boolean` | no | Indicates whether a backup repository must be updated. |
| `outOfSpaceInDays` | `integer(int32)` | no | Number of days before a backup repository runs out of free space. |
| `state` | `enum("Unknown", "Ok", "Inaccessible", "Disconnected", "OutOfDate", "Warning")` | no | State of a backup repository. |
| `path` | `string` | no | Path to the folder where backup files are stored. |
| `oneBackupFilePerVm` | `boolean` | no | Indicates whether a separate backup file is created for every machine in a job. |
| `isReFs` | `boolean` | no | Indicates whether a backup repository stores files in the ReFS format. |
| `isImmutable` | `boolean` | no | Indicates whether immutability is enabled for a backup repository. |
| `immutabilityIntervalDays` | `integer(int32)` | no | Immutability period, in days. |

| `virtualDisks` | [`VmVirtualDisk[]`](#schema-VmVirtualDisk) | no | Array of virtual disks configured for a VM. |

| `storageLimitMb` | `integer(int64)` | no | Maximum amount of disk space that can be provided by an organization VDC, in MB. |
| `storageUsedMb` | `integer(int64)` | no | Amount of disk space consumed on an organization VDC, in MB. |

| `cloudDirectorId` | `integer(int64)` | no | ID assigned to a VMware Cloud Director server. |
| `organizationId` | `integer(int64)` | no | ID assigned to an organization. |

| field | type | required | description |

| `capacityBytes` | `integer(int64)` | no | Storage capacity of a scale-out backup repository, in bytes. |
| `freeSpaceBytes` | `integer(int64)` | no | Amount of free storage space on a scale-out backup repository, in bytes. |
| `runningTasks` | `integer(int32)` | no | Number of currently running tasks on a scale-out backup repository. |
| `outOfSpaceInDays` | `integer(int32)` | no | Estimated number of days before a scale-out backup repository runs out of free space. |
| `state` | `enum("Unknown", "Ok", "Inaccessible", "Disconnected", "OutOfDate", "Warning")` | no | State of a scale-out backup repository. |
| `scaleoutRepositoryPolicy` | `enum("Unknown", "Performance", "DataLocality")` | no | Type of the backup file placement policy. |
| `copyPolicy` | `boolean` | no | Indicates whether all backups are copied to object storage as soon as they are created. |
| `movePolicyInDays` | `integer(int32)` | no | Period after which inactive backup chains on a performance extent are moved to a capacity extent, in days. |
| `archivingPolicyInDays` | `integer(int32)` | no | Period after which inactive backup chains on a capacity extent are moved to an archive extent, in days. |
| `encryptArchivedData` | `boolean` | no | Indicates whether encryption is enabled for the archived data. |

<a id="schema-ScaleoutRepositoryInfoPage"></a>

| field | type | required | description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `items` | [`ScaleoutRepositoryInfo[]`](#schema-ScaleoutRepositoryInfo) | no |  |
| `totalCount` | `integer(int32)` | no |  |

| `port` | `integer(int32)` | no | Port used to access a host. |
| `connectionState` | `enum("Unknown", "Connected", "NotResponding", "Disconnected")` | no | Connection status of a host. |
| `powerState` | `enum("Unknown", "PoweredOn", "PoweredOff", "Standby")` | no | Power status of a host. |
| `vendor` | `string` | no | Host vendor. |
| `model` | `string` | no | Host model. |

| `memorySizeBytes` | `integer(int64)` | no | Amount of memory available on a host, in bytes. |
| `nicCount` | `integer(int32)` | no | Number of network interface controllers connected to a host. |
| `isMaintenanceModeEnabled` | `boolean` | no | Indicates whether a host is in the maintenance mode. |
| `memoryUsageMb` | `integer(int32)` | no | Host memory usage, in MB. |
| `cpuUsageMhz` | `integer(int32)` | no | Host CPU usage, in MHz. |
| `isVmotionEnabled` | `boolean` | no | Indicates whether VMware vSphere vMotion is enabled for a host. |

## 6. How to build a matching endpoint

Replicate these patterns so a new endpoint is consistent with the rest of the API:

1. **Path & method** — match the observed naming style (lowercase, camelOrPascal); use the standard verb for the action (GET read, POST create, PUT/PATCH update, DELETE remove).
2. **Auth** — require the `Bearer` security scheme like every other operation.
3. **Response envelope** — wrap the payload as `{ items, totalCount }` to match existing 2xx bodies.
4. **Status codes** — reuse the codes already in play: 200, 204, 400, 403, 422.
5. **Schemas** — reference existing component schemas ([§5](#schemas)) for inputs/outputs instead of inventing new shapes.
6. **List endpoints** — if returning a collection, include the same pagination params the API already uses ([§3](#conventions)).
